Oh sons of great fame, I have completed this book which lies behind the science of medicine in assembly, and have finished it for its explanations and by my statements. And it came to me in vision that I would complete this book for you, which is part of the work from hands, namely "surgery".
And for this reason that the work of hands is pressed in our region and is strange all around everywhere, it has been lost through science and decay, and nothing remains from the fires except small descriptions in books of the ancient ones who have moved their hands. Let us say in the introduction of this book that whoever is not knowledgeable of the things said here will, if he guards himself, avoid falling into error and will know those who are wise.
Once I have wanted to try many of these who refuse to learn this science, and abandon themselves without knowledge and experience.

and let the skilled hands bind the wound with strong ties, and do not leave it until it heals.
and command that he does not release it (from its position).
